 unhone kaha ki desh beyimaanon ko sweekaar nahin karegaa

 adhikariyon ne bataaya ki raily ko dekhte hue suraksha ke pukhta intjaam kiye gaye hai

 unhone bataaya ki pradhanmantri ke raily ground ko 25 sectoron main baantkar 102 magistrate or 200 se adhik varisht police adhikari tainaat kiye gaye
 According to BJP officials, the rally attracted around two lakh people from nearby areas including Rampur, Amroha, Sambhal and Bijnor
 raily ko pradesh adhyaksh keshav prasad maury, party upaadhyaksh tathaa pradesh prabharee om maathur ne bhi sambodhit kiya

 maanon ko bhi aaraam hoga

 bijli se kisaanon kii pani kii samasya dur hogi
 He said that governments are not there to make announcements, governments are meant to complete work after making announcements
 piem narendra modi ne madhya pradesh main vikaas ke kaam kaa zikr kiya

 piem modi ne kaha ki madhya pradesh ke kisaanon ne pani kii kami ke baavjood doguna utpaadan kar desh kii tarakkee main yogadan diya he
 Speaking on the politics of UP, PM Modi said that you have seen the governments that work for their own people, but only BJP will bring a government that will work for the people
 piem modi ne kaha ki bhrashtachar is desh kii sarvaadhik museebaton kii jad main he

 bhrashtachar ke khilaaf ladaai ladane ke liye kuch log mujhe gunaahagaar kah rahe hai

 piem modi ne kaha ki notebandi ke baad amir garib ke pair pakad rahaa he
 They cannot go to the bank

 piem modi ne kaha, jandhan khaataa logon ke kaam aa rahaa he

 lekin ab yah sab kataren samaapt ho gai hai

 main ise sahi karne main laga hum

 upi kii raajnneeti par bolte hue piem modi ne kaha ki apane-apano ke liye kaam karne vaali sarkarein aapane dekhi hai, lekin keval bijepi hi aisi sarkaar laaegi jo logon ke liye kaam karegi

 ) The terrorist organization tehreek-e-taliban Pakistan has claimed responsibility for the attack on Bacha Khan University located near Peshawar
 yah vahi aatanki sanghathan he, jisane 2014 main peshawar ke army skool par hamalaa karke kai maasoom bacchon ko maut kii neend sula diya tha
 Let's know about this terrorist organization
 taharik-e-taliban kaa matlabataharik-e-taliban pakistanka matlab he 'pakistani chaatro kaa abhiyaan'
 'talib' means 'student' or 'seeker of religious education' and 'tehreek' means 'campaign' or 'campaign'
 yah ek sangh-shasit janajaatiy kshetra se ubharne vaala aatankwaadi sanghathan he
 It is different from the Taliban of Afghanistan
 haalanki yah sanghathan unki vichaardhaara kaa samarthan karata he
 The purpose of the TTP is to establish a radical Islamic regime based on Sharia in Pakistan
 isaki sthapana disambar 2007 main 13 aatanki guton ne milakar kii thi
 In January 2013, the tehreek-e-taliban announced that it wanted Sharia-based governance in India as well
 usne loktantr or dharm-nirpekshata khatm karne ke liye ladane kii baat bhi kahi thi
 This is the reason why this terrorist organization has been trying to be active in Kashmir
 maulanaa fajalullah he titipi kaa mukhiyaaise aatanki sanghathan ke duusare mukhiya hakimullah mahsood kii maut ke baad moulana fajalullah ne is sanghathan kii kaman sanbhali
 Maulna Fazlullah is considered special of Mehsud, the founder of this organization
 sanghathan main aatank ke dam par jagah banane vaale fajalullah ko november 2013titipika teesraa mukhiya chunaa gaya tha
 It was founded by Baitullah Mehsud, notorious as Pakistan Taliban, this organization was founded by the infamous Pakistani terrorist Baitullah Mehsud, who died on August 23, 2009
 titipi kaa thikaana pakistan-afghanistan seemaa par maujuud adivasee kshetra main he
